Briefly, a CHO cell line (CHO-N2) was established which expressed both a full-length human Notch2 cDNA, and p10xCBF1-luc. 2 × 104 CHO-N2 cells were plated per well into 96-well plates, and left to adhere for 2 hours. Notch signalling was activated by plating an additional CHO line which stably expresses full-length human Delta1 (CHO-hDelta1) onto the CHO-N2 cells.
